00003 /* This file contains 21200 polinomials, that is all primitive polynomials
00004    modulo two up to degree 18. Another version does contain
00005    8129334 polinomials, that is all primitive polynomials
00006    modulo two up to degree 27. Both are slightly edited versions of
00007    PrimitivePolynomialsModuloTwoUpToDegree27.c
00008 
00009    © 2002 "Monte Carlo Methods in Finance"

00018    =========================================================================
00019 */
